// Build a 32-bit Galois LFSR with taps at bit positions 32, 22, 2, and 1.

// Hint: This is long enough that you'd want to use vectors, not 32 instantiations of DFFs.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,    // Active-high synchronous reset to 32'h1
    output [31:0] q
);
   reg [31:q][0] lfsr;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            lfsr <= 32'h1;
        end else begin
            lfsr <= {lfsr[30:0], lfsr[31] ^ lfsr[21] ^ lfsr[1] ^ lfsr[0]};
        end
    end

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,    // Active-high synchronous reset to 32'h1
    output [31:0] q
);
   reg[31:0 q];
    
    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            q <= 32'h1;
        end else begin
            q <= {q[30:0], q[31] ^ q[21] ^ q[1] ^ q[0]};
        end
    end

endmodule

// Hint: This is long enough that you'd want to use vectors, not 32 instantiations of DFFs.

module top_module(

module top_module(
    input clk,

// Hint: This is long enough that you'd want to use vectors, not 32 instantiations of DFFs.

    input clk,

// Build a 32-bit Galois LFSR with taps at bit positions 32, 22, 2, and 1.

// Hint: This is long enough that you'd want to use vectors, not 32 instantiations of DFFs.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,    // Active-high synchronous reset to 32'h1
    output [31:0] q
);
   reg [31:1] q;;0;1reg [31:0] q_reg;
   wire feedback;

   assign feedback = q_reg[31] ^ q_reg[21] ^ q_reg[1] ^ q_reg[0];

   always @(posedge clk) begin
       if (reset) begin
           q_reg <= 32'h1;
       end else begin
           q_reg <= {q_reg[30:0], feedback};

   end

// Build a 32-bit Galois LFSR with taps at bit positions 32, 22, 2, and 1.

// Hint: This is long enough that you'd want to use vectors, not 32 instantiations of DFFs.

module top_module(
    input clk,
    input reset,    // Active-high synchronous reset to 32'h1
    output [31:0] q
);
   reg [31:1] q;;0; always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
